## that's right; correct
### mÃ©i cuÃ²
---
- **definition:** that's right; correct
- **pinyin:** mÃ©i cuÃ²
- **components:**
  - æ²¡(æ²’)
    - mÃ©i
    - no; not; have not; drown
  - é”™(éŒ¯)
    - cuÃ²
    - wrong; mistake; fault; error
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** æ²’(æ²’) (mÃ©i, "no; not") + éŒ¯(éŒ¯) (cuÃ², "wrong; mistake") suggests a negation of error, effectively conveying the idea of correctness or affirmation.
  - **interpretation:** The phrase æ²¡é”™(æ²’éŒ¯) (mÃ©i cuÃ², "that's right; correct") is used to affirm or confirm a statement, indicating that there is no error or mistake in what was said. It combines the negation 'æ²¡(æ²’)' (mÃ©i, "no; not") with 'é”™(éŒ¯)' (cuÃ², "wrong; mistake") to produce a positive affirmation.
- **examples:**
  - ä»–è¯´çš„æ²¡é”™(ä»–èªªçš„æ²’éŒ¯)ã€‚
